<form uuid="Ia396bc80181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.name.block><name>BYLAWS OF <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr></name></form.name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>I</designator><name>NAME AND HEADQUARTERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Name.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The name of the cooperative shall be <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of cooperative&rsqb;</inline.instr>, referred to in these bylaws as &ldquo;Cooperative.&rdquo;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Headquarters.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The headquarters of the cooperative shall be located at <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of cooperative&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>II</designator><name>FUNCTIONS AND OBJECTIVES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Business.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The business to be carried on by the cooperative shall be <inline.instr>&lsqb;description of business&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Other Objectives.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Other objectives of the cooperative shall be:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>cooperative service for the benefit of the members and of the consuming public;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>affiliation or cooperation with other cooperative organizations of a like nature in the local community, the state, the nation and other countries;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>promotion of the cooperative ideal through educational activities; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>such other objectives as may be set out in the certificate of incorporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item></form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>III</designator><name>MEMBERSHIP</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Eligibility.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Any person, irrespective of age, sex, race, nationality, political opinion, or religious belief, and any firm, partnership, or corporation, including both landlords and tenants in share tenancies, who is engaged in the production of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of agricultural product&rsqb;</inline.instr> in the territory in which the corporation is engaged in business, who agrees to be a patron of the corporation, and who pays such membership fees and meets such other conditions as may be prescribed by the board of directors is eligible to become a member of this cooperative.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Number.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The number of members of the corporation shall be limited to <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Fees, operating, and other charges.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Fee Required.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Each person on becoming a member of the corporation will pay to the corporation a fee of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of fee&rsqb;</inline.instr>, of which amount &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of annual subscription&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall be in payment of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of years&rsqb;</inline.instr> year&apos;s subscription to <inline.instr>&lsqb;&lsqb;name of publication&rsqb;/&lsqb;name of other similar publication of cooperative&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr> and the balance of which shall be applied to <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of intended use of balance amount&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The corporation&apos;s operating expenses shall be met by a percentage charged on returns for products sold and by a percentage charged on supplies purchased, the amount of such charges to be fixed by the board of directors. Payment for the expenses will be made on the first day of each month.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Payment of Fee and Membership Shares.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The fee must be paid in cash. A membership share may be paid for by:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Payments in lawful money of the United States;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Application of patronage refund;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(3)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Credit of interest of other debts due; or</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(4)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Any combination of the above.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item></form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Property Rights of Members.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The corporation will not have any capital stock. The following membership rights, privileges and restrictions shall apply:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>A member shall be entitled to only one vote and that only after the member has purchased one membership share. The full &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of fee&rsqb;</inline.instr> must be paid (see Subsection 3b above) within a period of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of months&rsqb;</inline.instr> months from the date of application. On failure to make such timely payment, the amount of the member&apos;s credit shall, at the discretion of the board of directors and after <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days&apos; notice by <inline.instr>&lsqb;registered mail/&lsqb;specification of mode of delivery&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr> to the member at the member&apos;s last-known address, be refunded and the membership cancelled. If a member cannot be located, the amount shall be applied to the work of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of committee&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Each member&apos;s patronage refund and share dividends shall be credited to the member as payment on membership shares until the member owns <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of shares&rsqb;</inline.instr> shares, and thereafter the member&apos;s patronage refunds and share dividends, if their combined total is &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of combined total&rsqb;</inline.instr> or more, shall be paid in cash unless the member gives other directions, provided, however, that the patronage refund shall be paid in the manner and to the extent required by the Internal Revenue Code and Treasury Department Regulations to qualify for income tax deductions or exclusions for this cooperative. Patronage refunds and share dividends not paid out shall be applied toward purchase of additional shares.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Dividends shall be paid on membership shares as provided below and shall accrue from the first day of the first full month during which a member owns at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of membership shares&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership shares. For all purposes relating to the payment of dividends, all shares purchased by a member not later than the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of any month shall be deemed to have been owned by the member on the first day of that month.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>d</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>A member may not hold more than <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of total membership shares&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the total of all membership shares issued and outstanding at any one time.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>e</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Membership shares are nontransferable except within a member&apos;s family and then only on approval of the board of directors after written request for such transfer.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>f</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The board of directors may, after written notice by first class mail, recall, at par value, the membership shares and terminate the membership of any member who has failed to patronize or participate in the organizational activities of the cooperative for at least one year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>g</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>For the purpose of this paragraph, &ldquo;family&rdquo; shall be defined as those individuals living in one household as the single purchasing unit. Individuals wishing to be grouped in such purchasing unit must so inform the cooperative in writing.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>h</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Each person who becomes or remains a member of this cooperative after the adoption of this bylaw (ARTICLE III, Section 4h) consents to include in <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her&rsqb;</inline.instr> gross income for federal income tax purposes the amount of any patronage refund paid to him or her by this cooperative by written notice of allocation (as defined in the Internal Revenue Code), except to the extent that such a patronage refund is not income to the member because: (1) it is attributable to the purchase of personal, living, or family items; or (2) it should be properly treated as an adjustment to the tax basis of property previously purchased. The term &ldquo;patronage refund&rdquo; as used herein shall have the same meaning as that term is used in the Internal Revenue Code.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Liability for Debts of Cooperative.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Membership shares are nonassessable. A member of this cooperative shall not be liable for the debts of the corporation to an amount exceeding the sum remaining unpaid on the membership fee or subscription to the capital stock, including any unpaid balance on any promissory notes given in payment.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Withdrawal of Amounts Credited on Purchase of Membership Shares.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>A member may withdraw, partially or wholly, amounts credited toward the purchase of membership shares, subject to the following provisions:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Member must submit written notice to the cooperative of intent to withdraw share credits.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Complete withdrawal necessitates resignation from membership.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Resignation from membership is effective when approved by the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>d</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Partial withdrawal is permitted only if at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of membership shares to be retained&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership shares are retained.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>e</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Credits shall be reduced proportionately if the total membership share credits of all members are impaired.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>f</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Member agrees to accept payment in goods or services purchased from the cooperative or in cash at the election of the cooperative.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>g</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Payment shall be made within one year from date of receipt of notice of intent, providing such payment will not, in the opinion of the board of directors, unduly impair the finances of the cooperative.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Suspension or Termination.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>If, following a hearing, the board of directors finds that a member has ceased to be an eligible member; has not, for a period of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of years&rsqb;</inline.instr> years, marketed through the corporation the products covered by the marketing agreement or agreements with the corporation or has not otherwise patronized the corporation; has moved out of the territory in which the corporation is operating; or has died or has withdrawn or resigned from the corporation, the board may suspend such member&apos;s rights as a member or terminate the membership. On termination of membership in the corporation, the membership certificate will be cancelled, all rights and interests of such member in the corporation will cease, and the member will be entitled only to payment or credit for the equitable appraised value of the member&apos;s property rights and interests in the corporation, as conclusively determined by the board of directors. In determining property rights and interests, all amounts allocated to each member or evidenced by certificates of any kind will be excluded, and any such amounts will be accounted for to members in accordance with the applicable terms and conditions. No action taken under this section will impair the obligations or liabilities of either party under any contract with the corporation, which may be terminated only as provided in these bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Method of Resignation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>After a person has been a member of the corporation for <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of years&rsqb;</inline.instr> years, the member may withdraw or resign from the corporation in any year on the last day of the anniversary month in which such member was accepted as a member by notifying the corporation of the intention to withdraw or resign, such notice to be given between the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> and the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> of the month immediately prior to the effective date of withdrawal or resignation. If the member fails to withdraw or resign in any year, as stated above, it is agreed that such failure will constitute conclusive evidence that the member has renewed membership in the corporation for another year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IV</designator><name>BUSINESS PRINCIPLES AND PRACTICES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Governing Principles.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The business of this cooperative shall be conducted according to the following principles:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Democratic control.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>There shall be one vote for each member. Voting by proxy is not permitted.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Open membership.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Membership is open to all producers of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of agricultural product&rsqb;</inline.instr> acting in good faith without regard to age, sex, race, nationality, political opinion, or religious belief.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Limited dividends on capital.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>In accordance with New York laws governing cooperative corporations, dividends on membership shares, if earned and declared, shall not exceed <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of maximum dividends on membership shares&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; per year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>d</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Cash sales at prevailing prices.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Goods and services shall be supplied to patrons at prevailing prices of the neighborhood. All sales shall be on a cash basis.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>e</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Patronage refunds based on purchases.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The distribution of all patronage refunds shall be on the basis of amount of purchases.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>f</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Education and promotion.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Funds shall be provided for education and promotion.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Net Surplus Savings and Earnings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>At the end of each fiscal year, the net surplus savings and earnings of the cooperative (referred to as net earnings) shall be determined and applied as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Capital shall be restored to the extent of any impairment thereof.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>An amount equal to <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of net earnings&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of net earnings shall be set aside as a reserve fund until such fund shall equal an amount representing <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of total membership shares outstanding&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the total membership shares outstanding.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Dividends at the rate of <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage rate of dividends&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; per annum shall be paid on membership certificates to all members who own at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of membership certificates&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership certificates, provided, however, that not more than <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of net earnings&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the net earnings shall be paid out as dividends on membership shares. In the event <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of net earnings&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the net earnings is insufficient to pay dividends as provided above at the rate of <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage rate of dividends&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt;, the rate shall be determined by dividing a sum equal to <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of net earnings&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the net earnings by the aggregate face value of all certificates on which dividends are payable under these bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>d</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Patronage refunds shall be paid as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Patronage refunds shall be paid on recorded sales. The board of directors shall, from time to time, provide the method and procedure by which business transacted with the cooperative by its patrons shall be recorded by the cooperative. Each patron shall be responsible for meeting all requirements as established pertaining to participation in keeping such patronage records. The sales and other business transactions so entered in the patronage records of the cooperative shall constitute recorded sales.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The amount available for payment of such refunds shall be: (a) that proportion of net earnings which the &ldquo;recorded sales&rdquo; of the cooperative bears to the total sales of the cooperative for the fiscal year; or (b) total net earnings for the fiscal year, less the amount paid to the restoration of capital, the reserve fund, and the payment of dividends on membership certificates, as required by law or by these bylaws, whichever is the smaller.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(3)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The rate or percentage of such refunds shall be determined by dividing the amount available for payment of refunds by the recorded sales of the cooperative for the fiscal year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(4)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>On written authorization from a member, &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of sum payable&rsqb;</inline.instr> of the sum payable to such member as dividends or as a patronage refund at the end of any fiscal year may be retained by the cooperative in payment of a year&apos;s subscription to &ldquo;<inline.instr>&lsqb;name of publication&rsqb;</inline.instr>&rdquo; or other similar publication of the cooperative.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VII</designator><name>DIRECTORS AND OFFICERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Number of Directors; Election.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The board of directors shall consist of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members. Each director shall be a member of the corporation in good standing, and a person will not be eligible to become a director if he or she is in competition with or is affiliated with any enterprise that is in competition with the corporation. Each year at the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership meeting, <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> directors shall be elected from the nominees presented by the nominating committee or from the floor, each for a term of one year or until a successor is elected. Any member with voting rights is eligible for directorship except employees and members of their immediate families. At least two nominees will be nominated for each directorship. All directors will be elected by secret ballot and the nominee with the greatest number of votes will be elected.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Alternate Members.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Each year at the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> meeting of the membership, there shall also be elected <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of alternate members&rsqb;</inline.instr> alternate members of the board. These members shall be the next <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of remaining members&rsqb;</inline.instr> remaining nominees for the board of directors having the highest vote after all vacancies on the board of directors have been filled. They shall have the privilege of participating in the discussion but have no power to vote. In case of an absence of a regular director at a given board meeting, the chairperson shall appoint the alternate present who received the highest number of votes to function as a director at the meeting. If a second regular director is absent from the given board meeting, the chairperson shall appoint the alternate present who received the second highest number of votes to function as a director at such meeting. Should a third regular director be absent from the given board meeting, the chairperson shall appoint the alternate who received the third highest number of votes to function as a director at such meeting. In case of a vacancy on the board, the board shall select one of the alternates to serve during the vacancy but not beyond the next <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Meetings; Quorum.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The directors shall have regular monthly meetings, and <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall constitute a quorum for official business. A majority of the <inline.instr>&lsqb;total number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> directors is required for official action. All meetings shall be open to the members of the cooperative.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Absence from Meetings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Any director who is absent from <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of consecutive meetings&rsqb;</inline.instr> consecutive meetings of the board shall be dropped from the board at the next meeting unless excused by vote of the board, provided that the director shall have been notified of the situation by the secretary, such notice to be given after a director has missed <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of consecutive meetings&rsqb;</inline.instr> consecutive meetings.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Special Meetings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>A special meeting of the board of directors will be held whenever called by the president or by a majority of the directors. Any business may be transacted at a special meeting. Each call for a special meeting will be in writing, signed by the person or persons calling for the meeting, addressed and delivered to the secretary, and will state the time and place of the meeting. On the signing of a waiver of notice of a meeting, a meeting of the board of directors may be held at any time.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Compensation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The compensation, if any, of the members of the board of directors and of the executive committee will be determined by the members of the corporation at any regular or special meeting of the corporation. No member of the board of directors will occupy any position in the corporation on regular salary. The compensation, if any, of the corporation&apos;s officers will be determined by <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of determination method&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Election of Officers.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>At the first meeting of the directors after each <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership meeting, the directors shall elect as officers of the cooperative <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: from among the directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> a president and a vice president. The directors shall also elect a treasurer and a secretary (or a secretary&ndash;-treasurer), who may, but need not, be members of the board or members of the cooperative.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of Officers.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The duties of the officers shall be as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the president.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The president shall preside over all meetings of the corporation and of the board of directors; call special meetings of the board of directors, as required; perform all acts and duties and render such reports as are usually required of an executive and presiding officer; sign certificates for shares or membership of the corporation and such other documents as the president may be authorized or directed to sign by the board of directors; and perform such other duties as the board of directors may prescribe.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the vice president.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>In the absence of disability of the president, the vice president shall perform the duties of the president.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the secretary.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The secretary shall keep a record of all meetings of the corporation and of the board of directors; keep complete membership records and have general charge of the corporation&apos;s books and records; sign all membership or stock certificates with the president and sign such other papers as the secretary may be authorized or directed to sign by the board of directors; serve all notices required by law and these bylaws and make all reports required by law; keep the corporate seal and all books of blank certificates complete; and affix the corporate seal to all papers requiring such seal.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the treasurer.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The treasurer will perform such duties with respect to the finances of the corporation as may be prescribed by the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>9</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Powers of Directors.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The board of directors shall have full power in administrating the cooperative&apos;s affairs and may make such rules and regulations with respect to the business and employees of the cooperative as the board deems advisable, provided that all actions shall be consistent with these bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>10</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Committees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The president shall appoint the following standing committees of the board immediately after taking office: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of standing committees&rsqb;</inline.instr>, as well as such other special committees as may be deemed necessary by the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>11</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Loans Involving Mortgages.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The board shall not accept any loan involving a mortgage on any of the property of the cooperative, except as authorized at a membership meeting with previous notice of the proposed loan.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>12</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Other Loans.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The cooperative, by action of the board of directors, may accept other loans, provided such loans do not in the aggregate exceed the cooperative&apos;s net worth, except as authorized at a membership meeting with previous notice of the proposed loan or by mail ballot.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Loans from members and others shall be solicited only when sufficient capital cannot be obtained from membership shares.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>13</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Bonds.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Fidelity bonds shall be required of the treasurer and manager.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>14</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Suggested Order of Business.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Suggested order of business at regular meetings of the directors is:</form.text></form.para>

<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Minutes of the preceding meeting</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Unfinished business</form.text></form.para></form.item>

</form.unit></form.item></form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VIII</designator><name>NOMINATIONS AND ELECTIONS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Limitation on Consecutive Terms.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>No member shall be elected as a director for more than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of consecutive full terms&rsqb;</inline.instr> consecutive full terms.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Nominating Committee.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>A nominating committee of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members shall be elected annually at the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Nominations by Committee.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The nominating committee shall make nominations for all positions, whether as regular or alternate directors, to be filled by election of the members. It shall submit a list of such nominations, the number of which shall be at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of total number of positions to be filled&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; greater than the total number of positions to be filled, to the secretary of the cooperative by the <inline.instr>&lsqb;day of week&rsqb;</inline.instr> following the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> <inline.instr>&lsqb;day of week&rsqb;</inline.instr> of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr>. The committee may not nominate any of its own members. Such members may, however, be nominated by petition or from the floor, as provided by Section 4 of this ARTICLE.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Nomination by Members.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Nominations may also be made by petition of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> or more members submitted to the secretary of the cooperative by the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> in any year. Such nominees will be provided equal opportunity with other nominees to present their views. Each voting member of record shall be notified of all nominations not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days before an election is held and shall be informed which nominations were made by the committee and which by petition. Additional nominations may be made from the floor.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IX</designator><name>MANAGERS AND EMPLOYEES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Manager&apos;s Authority.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The manager shall be in full charge of the business of the cooperative but shall conduct the business in conformity with policies determined by the board of directors and the membership and in accordance with regulations and instructions of the board of directors as the administrative agency of the cooperative.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Reports to Board; Financial Statements.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The manager shall attend all meetings of the board of directors and shall make such reports as are desired by the board. The manager shall prepare and submit a monthly financial statement to the board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Report to Membership; Inventories.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The manager shall attend membership meetings and make such reports as are requested by the president or by action taken in membership meetings. In <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month of semi-annual inventory&rsqb;</inline.instr>, the manager shall take a complete inventory. At the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> meeting of the directors and at the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership meeting, the manager shall present a statement of operations and a balance sheet. At the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> meeting of the directors and the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership meeting, the manager shall make corresponding reports for the year. In each case, the manager shall have available copies for inspection by anyone interested, and a permanent copy shall be filed in the cooperative&apos;s registered office.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Employee Grievances.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Any employee or representative of the employees shall have the right to present any grievances directly to the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Suspension of Employees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The manager must give an employee <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days&apos; notice of intention of terminating that employee&apos;s services. For serious cause, such as dishonesty or other immoral conduct, the board of directors may immediately suspend an employee. In either case, the employee shall have the right of a hearing before the board and the right of appeal from the decision of the board as provided in Section 4 of ARTICLE X on initiative and referendum. This section shall be subject to any agreement that this cooperative shall have entered into with any labor union.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>X</designator><name>PATRONS AND PATRONS&apos; NET MARGINS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Patrons.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Each patronage transaction between this corporation and each patron will be subject to and will include as a part of its terms each provision of this ARTICLE X, whether it be expressly referred to in the transaction or not, and no person shall have any authority to transact any business for this corporation with any patron on any terms inconsistent with this ARTICLE X. On selling, consigning, or otherwise delivering any agricultural product to this corporation or contracting to do so and on buying or otherwise receiving any farm supplies or equipment from this corporation or contracting to do so, each patron, with or without then executing any writing or doing any other act, thereby:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Shall, as further consideration due the patron from this corporation on account of such transaction, become entitled to have paid such proportion of the patrons&apos; net margins received by this corporation as such patronage bears to the aggregate patronage of all patrons, as is in this document more particularly defined and provided; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Shall, in consideration of similar agreements by others in the same fiscal year, promise and agree to invest in the capital of this corporation (revolving fund) as requested by the board of directors <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of determinant&rsqb;</inline.instr> of the agricultural products sold, consigned, or otherwise delivered to the corporation, which amount is made deductible from the sales proceeds otherwise payable to the patron, and, in addition, such further sum or sums of money as the board of directors may specify, provided, however, that the patron&apos;s obligation to invest in the capital in any fiscal year of this corporation, in addition to the rate prescribed above, shall be limited to an amount equal to the patron&apos;s share of such patrons&apos; net margins for the fiscal year next preceding the fiscal year in which such investment is required and shall be proportionate to the investments required of other patrons. It is the intention and agreement of this corporation and its patrons with each other that, as the board of directors shall deem the capital to be necessary to repurchase or retire previously issued certificates of indebtedness or capital interests, its several patrons shall, subject to the foregoing limitations, furnish such additional capital as may be required and shall do so substantially in proportion to their respective patronage in the preceding fiscal year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Computation of Patrons&apos; Net Margins.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The patrons&apos; net margins, calculated on the basis of each fiscal year, shall be computed as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Gross receipts.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>All proceeds of all sales of products marketed for patrons, plus all sums received for supplies and equipment procured for patrons, plus all sums received from all other sources except loans or contributions to this corporation or investments in its capital, will be deemed to be the &ldquo;gross receipts.&rdquo;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Patrons&apos; net margins.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>This corporation will deduct from the gross receipts the sum of the following items:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>All costs and expenses and other charges that are lawfully excludible or deductible from this corporation&apos;s gross receipts for the purpose of determining the amount of any net margin of this corporation; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>An amount equal to <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of balance of gross receipts&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the balance of the gross receipts that remain after first having deducted from it the items referred to in Clause (1).</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>If, in any fiscal year, this corporation incurs a net operating loss that is recognizable for tax purposes, the board of directors will have full authority to charge off such loss against net margins of future years or against revolving fund credits or in such other manner as will afford the corporation the maximum benefit for tax purposes.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The balance of the gross receipts that remain after the foregoing deductions will be deemed to be the &ldquo;patrons&apos; net margins.&rdquo;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The amount deducted pursuant to Clause (2) above will be set aside in a reserve and apportioned to patrons in accordance with their patronage during the fiscal year, provided that, when the reserve reaches the sum of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of reserves&rsqb;</inline.instr>, the board of directors in its discretion may either: (a) make no further deductions; or (b) retire such amounts of the reserve as it considers may be in excess of the corporation&apos;s reserve needs. Such retirement will be accomplished by paying off in full or pro rata patrons&apos; apportioned interests, by years, the oldest being paid first.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>The patrons&apos; respective shares of the patrons&apos; net margins will be computed on the basis of their respective patronage of, and the net margins resulting from the operations of, the various pools or departments of this corporation and will be in proportion to the quantity or value of the products delivered by, or supplies or equipment procured for, such patrons.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Payment of Patrons&apos; Net Margins.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Each patron&apos;s share of the patrons&apos; net margins will be payable to the patron in cash at the close of each fiscal year, but the legal offset of the payments due a patron against the obligation of such patron to subscribe for capital, as provided in Section 1(b) of this ARTICLE X, will constitute full and complete discharge of the obligation of the corporation to make payment as provided in these bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Lien.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>This corporation will have a first lien on the interest of each patron in the patrons&apos; net margins for all indebtedness of such patron to this corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XI</designator><name>REVOLVING FUND</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Purpose.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>This corporation will establish and maintain a revolving fund for the purpose of acquiring and maintaining adequate capital to finance its business.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Investment in Fund.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>This corporation may require investment in its revolving fund as provided in ARTICLE X, Section 1(b) of these bylaws. Proper entries will be made on the corporation&apos;s books and records so that the new credit to each holder of an interest in the revolving fund in each year can be ascertained at any time. This corporation may issue revolving fund certificates to evidence credits in such fund, and the certificates may be in such form and contain such terms and conditions not inconsistent with this ARTICLE XI as the board of directors may prescribe.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Operation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Investments in the revolving fund need not be segregated from, but on the contrary may be invested in or commingled with, any other assets of this corporation. No dividend, interest, or any other income will be declared or paid on account of any net credits in the revolving fund. This corporation will have a first lien on each revolving fund credit for all indebtedness of the holder thereof to this corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Repayment.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>When, in the judgment of the board of directors, the net balance in the revolving fund exceeds the amount of capital reasonably needed by the corporation, it will apply such excess to the retirement, in full or pro rata, of all the net credits in the revolving fund, provided that such certificates will be retired in the order of issuance by years and there will be no discrimination between investments received in the same fiscal year. Notwithstanding any other provision of this section, the board of directors, in its discretion, may retire any net credits at any time when the holder: (a) dies; (b) otherwise ceases to be a producer; or (c) moves from the territory served by the corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Transfer.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Any assignment or transfer of any revolving fund will not be binding on this corporation without the consent of the board of directors or until it shall have been entered in the books of this corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XII</designator><name>INITIATIVE, REFERENDUM, AND RECALL</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Regulations for Mail Ballots.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Regulations for conducting mail ballots under this section shall be made by the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Petition for Director&apos;s Recall; Balloting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Any director may be recalled by the following method: On petition of at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of voting members&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the voting members, accompanied by written charges, the secretary or other officer specified in the petition shall conduct a recall election at a regular or special meeting. The ballot shall contain two statements of not more than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of words&rsqb;</inline.instr> words each, one by a proponent and one by an opponent of the recall. The director against whom the charges have been brought must be given at least 20-days written notice of the time, place, and object of any such meeting and of the charges to be brought, and the director shall be given an opportunity to be heard at the meeting and to present and cross-examine witnesses. A three-fourths vote of at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of voting members&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the entire membership shall determine the election.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Referendum on Certain Motions.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>On demand of one-third of the entire board of directors made immediately and so recorded at the same meeting at which the original motion was passed, any matter that has been approved or passed on by the board must be referred to the entire membership for a decision at the next regular or special meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XIII</designator><name>AMENDMENTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Proposal.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Amendments to these bylaws may be proposed:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>By the board of directors, acting on its own motion or on the petition of any member, provided that if such a petition is signed by at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members and submitted to the board of directors at a board meeting not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days before a membership meeting, the board of directors must submit the proposed amendment to the members by mail, as provided below, and the proposed amendment must be voted on at the next membership meeting; or</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>By any member submitting the proposed amendment in writing supported by a petition of at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members at any regular membership meeting. The board of directors must notify the membership of the proposed amendment at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr>-days prior to the next membership meeting, and the proposed amendment must be voted on at the next membership meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Adoption.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>Amendment to these bylaws may be adopted by the written consent of members entitled to exercise a majority of the voting power or by the vote of a majority of a quorum at a meeting of members duly called. Such meeting shall be considered duly called if the proposed amendment has been submitted in writing at the next preceding regular membership meeting or has been submitted to the members by mail at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr>-days prior to the membership meeting at which a vote on the amendment is taken.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XIV</designator><name>DISSOLUTION</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><form.text>This cooperative may be dissolved only by a <inline.instr>&lsqb;fraction of votes&rsqb;</inline.instr> vote of all voting members of the entire membership at any regular or special meeting when due notice of such action has been given in advance. On dissolution, any reserves of the cooperative in excess of its financial obligation, including debts and expenses, par value of invested capital paid on subscriptions, patronage dividends and membership capital, shall be turned over to such recognized cooperative organization as the membership may determine.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>

<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Sound tax planning for specialized entities such as a cooperative usually advocates inclusion in the articles of incorporation or bylaws of the goal of complying with the tax requirements. That demonstrates that the purpose of the entity is to meet the tax requirements and makes easier its claim to the specialized tax treatment afforded by the Internal Revenue Code. As an example, the key to allowance of the patronage dividend exclusion is a pre-existing enforceable obligation of the co-op to distribute its patronage earnings among its patrons. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1388" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;1388(a)(2)</cite>. Listing this in the bylaws not only shows that the corporation plans to do this but also makes it a pre-existing obligation of the corporation. If this should not be covered elsewhere, it nevertheless provides compliance with the Code.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Further examples of the policy of covering tax requirements in the bylaws may be found in the foregoing bylaws. See, for example, Sec 4(h) of ARTICLE III and Secs 1(c), (e), and (h) of ARTICLE IV.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Only persons engaged in the production of agricultural products, or cooperative corporations of such producers organized under the laws of this or any other state, shall be eligible for membership in any agricultural marketing or purchasing corporation formed or operated under the provisions of this Article. The terms and conditions of membership shall be prescribed in the bylaws. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="111">Coop. Corp. <item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>III.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>In accordance with provisions in the bylaws, any person shall: (1) forfeit his or her membership upon proof that he or she has ceased to be engaged in the occupation or occupations for the servicing of which the corporation was formed or has ceased to have the qualifications requisite for membership; and (2) upon such notice and terms as may be prescribed in the bylaws, surrender his or her membership certificate or his or her shares of stock upon payment of the par or otherwise designated value thereof and of any accrued dividends thereon, as may appear in the accounting at the end of the current fiscal year. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="42">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;42</cite>.</para.text></para>

<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Any member of a nonstock corporation may, subject to fulfilling the liability, contractual or otherwise, then incurred by him or her as a member of such corporation, resign and withdraw from such corporation, in accordance with provisions therefor in the bylaws. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="43">Coop. <para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Return on membership capital may not exceed 12&percnt; per year. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="111" subref="(a)">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;111(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>

<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Any corporation may, on resolution adopted by its board of directors, enter into all necessary and proper contracts and agreements with any other cooperative corporation or association. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="14" subref="(l)">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;14(l)</cite>.</para.text></para>

</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VII.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>The bylaws may provide for the qualifications, compensation, duties, and term of office of directors; the time of their election; and the mode and manner of giving notice. Directors shall be elected at the first annual meeting in three classes; the first class shall serve for a period of one year, the second class shall serve for two years, and the third class shall serve for three years. Thereafter, all successors will be elected for a period of three years. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="60">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;60</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>The first annual meeting must be held within a reasonable time so as to give the members or the shareholders an opportunity to elect their own board as promptly as possible, and a member or shareholder is entitled to an order compelling such meeting if necessary. <cite type="case">Lazar v. Knolls Co-op. Section No. 2, 205 Misc. 748, 130 N.Y.S.2d 407 (Sup 1954)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VII.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>The officers of every cooperative corporation must include a president, one or more vice presidents, secretary, and treasurer who are required to be elected annually by the board of directors. The president and a first vice president must be members of the corporation or of a member corporation and must be elected from among the directors. Other officers need not be directors or members of the corporation. The offices of secretary and treasurer may be combined. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="64">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;64</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="532, 536" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;532, 536</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VII.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>13.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Before handling funds or securities of the corporation, amounting to &dollar;1,000 or more in any one year, the officer or employee shall be covered by an adequate bond to be approved by the board of directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="65">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;65</cite>.</para.text></para>

<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>X.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>A cooperative that does not make full cash payment, utilizing instead qualified written notices of allocation (making at least 20&percnt; cash payment of the patronage dividend), must obtain the written consent of the recipient to take into account the stated dollar amount of the patronage distribution for federal income tax purposes. One method of obtaining such consent is through the cooperative adopting an appropriate bylaw and otherwise following the procedure laid down in the federal statutes. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1381">26 U.S.C.A. &dblsect;1381</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1382">1382</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1385">1385</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1388">1388</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Qualified written notice of allocation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="E-1121">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d &para;E-1121</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Noncash patronage dividends, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="5:18">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;5:18</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XII.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Any member may bring charges against a director by filing them in writing with the secretary, together with a petition signed by 5&percnt; of the members, requesting removal. The corporation may thereupon remove the director by the affirmative vote of three-fourths of the members voting thereon at a meeting promptly held after due notice in writing, setting forth accurately the purpose for which such meeting is called, provided that at such meeting not less than 10&percnt; of the entire membership vote, personally or by mail. The director involved shall be given a copy of the charges reasonably in advance of the meeting, and he or she and the complainant shall have an opportunity at the meeting to be heard in person or by counsel and to present and cross-examine witnesses. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="63">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;63</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>In case the bylaws provide for election of directors by districts with primary elections in each district, then the petition for removal of a director must be signed by 20&percnt; of the members residing in the district from which such director was elected. The board of directors must call a special meeting of the members residing in that district to consider the removal of the director, and, by a concurrent vote of a majority of the members of the district voting on the issue, the director will be removed from office. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="63">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;63</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="569">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;569</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XIII.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>The bylaws must provide a method for the bylaws to be amended, see <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="16">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;16</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>

<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="128">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;128</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>

<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XIV.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>A cooperative corporation may, at any meeting and upon due and express notice previously given, by vote of two-thirds of all of the members or stockholders voting thereon, discontinue its operations and settle its affairs. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="17">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;17</cite>.</para.text></para>

<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|23|32:23"><para.text>Under ARTICLE II., Section 1, description of business may include name of agricultural product.</para.text></para>
