<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia39758c0181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.name.block><name>BYLAWS OF <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF AGRICULTURAL COOPERATIVE ASSOCIATION&rsqb;</inline.instr>, A NEW YORK AGRICULTURAL COOPERATIVE ASSOCIATION</name></form.name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>I</designator><name>MEMBERS AND MEMBERSHIP</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Eligibility.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Persons engaged in the production of agricultural products and cooperative corporations may become shareholders of this corporation by purchasing at least one fully paid membership share and by agreeing to comply with the bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Termination of Membership.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Any shareholder may be expelled by the vote of a majority of the shareholders voting at a regular or special meeting, provided:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The notice of the meeting specifically states that the expulsion of the shareholder will be considered;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The shareholder whose expulsion is to be considered is notified in writing of that fact at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days in advance of the meeting by a notice sent by registered mail, postage prepaid, to the shareholder&apos;s last-known address as it appears on the corporation&apos;s records; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The shareholder is given an opportunity to be heard either in person or by counsel at the meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Expulsion may be for such cause as a majority of the shareholders voting at the meeting may deem sufficient. On expulsion of a shareholder, the corporation shall repurchase the membership shares held by the shareholder if and when, in the board of directors&apos; sole discretion, there are sufficient funds available.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>II</designator><name>MEETINGS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Regular.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>A regular meeting of the shareholders shall be held between the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day 1&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month 1&rsqb;</inline.instr> and the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day 2&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month 2&rsqb;</inline.instr> of each year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Special.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Special meetings of the shareholders may be called by the board of directors, and a special meeting must be called by the secretary in response to a petition signed by <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of shareholders&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the shareholders.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Notice.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Notice of all special meetings of shareholders shall be given at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days before the meeting by mailing a notice to each shareholder at the shareholder&apos;s last-known address.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Quorum.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>At any meetings of the shareholders, the presence in person of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of shareholders having voting rights&rsqb;</inline.instr> shareholders having voting rights or such lesser number of persons as shall equal <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of all shareholders having voting rights&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of all shareholders having voting rights constitutes a quorum for the transaction of business. If the written votes of absent shareholders are received and counted, the number of absent shareholders so voting shall be included in determining whether quorum requirements are satisfied with respect to matters upon which such votes are cast.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Voting Rights.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Each shareholder of the corporation is entitled to cast one vote and no more, regardless of the number of membership shares held by the shareholder. In the case of membership shares held in joint ownership by two or more persons, any one of such persons may cast the vote. Members may vote in person or by mail, subject to rules and regulations set forth by the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>III</designator><name>DIRECTORS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Conduct of Affairs.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Except as otherwise provided by the articles of incorporation or these bylaws, the powers of this corporation shall be exercised, its property controlled, and its affairs conducted by a board of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Election.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The persons named as directors shall serve until the first annual meeting of the shareholders. At that meeting, the shareholders shall nominate and elect <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> directors. In all cases, directors shall serve until their successors are elected.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Vacancies.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Any vacancy occurring in the board of directors, except by recall, shall be filled by appointment by a majority of the remaining board shareholders though they constitute less than a quorum. Any director so appointed shall hold office only until <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her&rsqb;</inline.instr> successor is elected at the next annual meeting of the shareholders.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Regular Meetings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The board of directors shall hold regular meetings at least once a month at a time and place previously determined by the board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Special Meetings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Special meetings may be called at any time by the board of directors. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Text percentage of members of shareholders&rsqb;</inline.instr> percent of the members of shareholders may file a petition stating the specific business to be brought before the corporation and demand a special meeting at any time. Such meeting must then be called by the directors. Notice of all special meetings, together with a statement of the purpose or purposes, must be mailed to each shareholder at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr>-days prior to the meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Quorum.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>At any meeting of the board of directors, <inline.instr>&lsqb;a majority of/&lsqb;fraction of directors&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr> directors shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of business.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Compensation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Directors and officers shall receive no compensation for performing the duties of their respective offices, except as authorized by the shareholders.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Removal of Directors.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Any shareholder may bring charges against a director by filing them in writing with the secretary of the corporation, together with a petition signed by <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of shareholders&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the shareholders, requesting the removal of the director in question. The removal shall be voted on at the next regular or special meeting of the corporation, and by a vote of three-fourths of the shareholders in attendance, provided that not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of entire membership vote&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the entire membership vote personally or by mail, the corporation may remove the director and fill the vacancy. The director against whom such charges have been brought will be informed in writing of the charges prior to the meeting and will have an opportunity at the meeting to be heard in person or by counsel and to present and cross examine witnesses, and the person bringing the charges against such director shall have the same opportunity.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IV</designator><name>OFFICERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Officers.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The officers shall be a president and a vice president, who shall be directors, and a secretary and a treasurer who need not be directors or shareholders of the cooperative. Their duties shall be as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the president.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The president shall preside over all meetings of the corporation and of the board of directors; call special meetings of the board of directors, as required; perform all acts and duties, and render such reports as are usually required of an executive and presiding officer; sign certificates for shares of the corporation and such other documents as the president may be authorized or directed to sign by the board of directors; and perform such other duties as the board of directors may prescribe.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the vice president.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>In the absence or disability of the president, the vice president shall perform the duties of the president.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the secretary.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The secretary shall keep a record of all meetings of the corporation and of the board of directors; keep complete membership records and have general charge of the corporation&apos;s books and records; sign all stock certificates with the president and sign such other papers as the secretary may be authorized or directed to sign by the board of directors; serve all notices required by law and these bylaws and make all reports required by law; and keep the corporate seal and all books of blank certificates complete and affix the corporate seal to all papers requiring such seal.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duties of the treasurer.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The treasurer will perform such duties with respect to the finances of the corporation as may be prescribed by the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Election.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Officers shall be elected annually by the board of directors at the first meeting of the shareholders.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Removal.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Any shareholder may bring charges against an officer by filing them in writing with the secretary of the corporation, together with a petition signed by <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of shareholders&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the shareholders, requesting the removal of the officer in question. The removal shall be voted on at the next regular or special meeting of the corporation, and by a vote of a majority of the shareholders, the corporation may remove the officer and fill the vacancy. The officer against whom such charges have been brought will be informed in writing of the charges prior to the meeting and will have an opportunity at the meeting to be heard in person or by counsel and to present witnesses, and the person bringing the charges against such director shall have the same opportunity.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Vacancies.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Any office that becomes vacant will be filled by election of the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>V</designator><name>ACCOUNTING</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Fiscal Year.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The books of the corporation shall be kept on the basis of a fiscal year ending on <inline.instr>&lsqb;end date of fiscal year&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Annual Audit.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The board of directors shall arrange for an annual audit of the books and records of the corporation by a certified public accountant.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VI</designator><name>MEMBERSHIP SHARES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Issuance.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>No share shall be issued until its par value has been paid in full. All shares shall be consecutively numbered in the name and address of each shareholder, together with the number of shares owned and the dates of issue, and shall be entered on the corporation&apos;s books.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Joint Ownership.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Membership shares may only be jointly owned by two or more persons.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Transfer of Shares.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Membership shares shall be nontransferable except to persons engaged in the production of agricultural products, and such restrictions shall be printed on every certificate of common stock.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Purchase by Corporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>The corporation has the right to cancel the membership and to purchase, at par value, the shares of any shareholder who has failed to patronize the corporation as a producer or consumer for a period of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days after giving <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr>-days&apos; notice by registered mail to the shareholder at the shareholder&apos;s last-known address. The corporation may also, in the discretion of the board of directors, purchase, at par value, all or part of the shares of a shareholder who makes a written request for such purchase. Sale to the corporation by any shareholder of all of such shareholder&apos;s shares will constitute resignation from membership.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VII</designator><name>DISTRIBUTION OF NET INCOME</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>Net income in excess of additions to reserves and surpluses shall be distributed to the shareholders of the cooperative on the basis of patronage by action of the board of directors. However, in accordance with state law governing cooperative corporations, dividends on membership stock, if earned and declared, shall not exceed <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of dividends&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; per year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VIII</designator><name>REFERENDUM</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>On demand of one-third of the entire board, made immediately and recorded at the same meeting at which the original motion was passed, any matter passed by the board must be referred to all shareholders for decision at the next regular or special meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IX</designator><name>AMENDMENTS TO BYLAWS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><form.text>A majority vote of a quorum of shareholders attending a meeting, of which notice of the proposed bylaws has been given, is sufficient to adopt or amend the bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>Sound tax planning for specialized entities such as a cooperative usually advocates inclusion in the articles of incorporation or bylaws of the goal of complying with the tax requirements. That demonstrates that the purpose of the entity is to meet the tax requirements and makes easier its claim to the specialized tax treatment afforded by the Internal Revenue Code. As an example, the key to allowance of the patronage dividend exclusion is a pre-existing enforceable obligation of the co-op to distribute its patronage earnings among its patrons. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1388" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;1388(a)(2)</cite>. Listing this in the bylaws not only shows that the corporation plans to do this but also makes it a pre-existing obligation of the corporation. If this should not be covered elsewhere, it nevertheless provides compliance with the Code.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>Cooperative corporations may issue either stock (as in these bylaws) or membership shares. For a form of bylaws containing membership provisions, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="32:23">&sect;32:23</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>Only persons engaged in the production of agricultural products, or cooperative corporations of such producers organized under the laws of this or any other state, shall be eligible for membership in any agricultural marketing or purchasing corporation formed or operated under the provisions of this Article. The terms and conditions of membership shall be prescribed in the bylaws. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="111" subref="(a)">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;111(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>

<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>I.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>In accordance with provisions in the bylaws, any person: (1) shall forfeit his or her membership upon proof that he or she has ceased to be engaged in the occupation or occupations for the servicing of which the corporation was formed or has ceased to have the qualifications requisite for membership; and (2) shall, upon such notice and terms as may be prescribed in the bylaws, surrender his or her membership certificate or his or her shares of stock upon payment of the par or otherwise designated value thereof and of any accrued dividends thereon, as may appear in the accounting at the end of the current fiscal year. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="42">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;42</cite>.</para.text></para>

</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>III.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>A cooperative corporation may provide a fair remuneration for its directors and for members of its executive committee. No director or member of the executive committee shall be a party to a contract for profit with the corporation that, in substance, shall differ in any way from similar contracts by it with members or with others or that shall vary from terms generally current in the district. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="62">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;62</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>

</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>III.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>Any member may bring charges against a director by filing them in writing with the secretary, together with a petition signed by 5&percnt; of the members, requesting removal. The corporation may thereupon remove the director by the affirmative vote of three-fourths of the members voting thereon at a meeting promptly held after due notice in writing, setting forth accurately the purpose for which such meeting is called, provided that at such meeting not less than 10&percnt; of the entire membership vote, personally or by mail. The director involved shall be given a copy of the charges reasonably in advance of the meeting, and he or she and the complainant shall have an opportunity at the meeting to be heard in person or by counsel and to present and cross-examine witnesses. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="63">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;63</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>In case the bylaws provide for election of directors by districts with primary elections in each district, then the petition for removal of a director must be signed by 20&percnt; of the members residing in the district from which such director was elected. The board of directors must call a special meeting of the members residing in that district to consider the removal of the director, and, by a concurrent vote of a majority of the members of the district voting on the issue, the director will be removed from office. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="63">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;63</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="569">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;569</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IV.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>The officers of every cooperative corporation must include a president, one or more vice presidents, secretary, and treasurer who are required to be elected annually by the board of directors. The president and a first vice president must be members of the corporation or of a member corporation and must be elected from among the directors. Other officers need not be directors or members of the corporation. The offices of secretary and treasurer may be combined. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="64">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;64</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="532, 536" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;532, 536</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IX.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|24|32:24"><para.text>For an agricultural cooperative corporation, the bylaws may provide for their amendment by the board of directors; however, any amendment adopted by the board that affects the preferential rights or obligations of the members or stockholders shall be reported to the next annual meeting of the corporation and, if not affirmatively approved thereat, shall cease to be in effect. Such bylaws reported to the annual meeting may be adopted, repealed, or amended on the affirmative vote of two-thirds of the members, stockholders, or delegates voting thereon at a meeting held after due written notice setting forth the proposed action and the purpose of the meeting. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="111">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;111</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="128">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;128</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
</item.reference.block>
</note.block>

<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:24.50</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Membership</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form>
<form.para><form.text>A membership in <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr> is defined as any person, firm, corporation or other organization whose members are engaged in <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of activity&rsqb;</inline.instr> provided the individual or corporation is contributing to or otherwise financially supporting the activities of this organization in a manner established and approved by the Board of Directors.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>Each member is entitled to one vote at the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr> membership meetings.</form.text></form.para>

<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|25|32:25"><form.text>These bylaws may be amended at any special or annual members&apos; meeting by two-thirds of the votes cast, provided that notice of the proposed alteration or amendment be contained in the notice of the meeting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|25|32:25"><form.text>These bylaws may be amended by the board of directors, provided, however, that any amendment adopted by the board that affects the preferential rights or obligations of the members or stockholders shall be reported to the next annual meeting of the corporation and, if not affirmatively approved thereat, shall cease to be in effect. Such bylaws reported to the annual meeting may be adopted, repealed, or amended on the affirmative vote of two-thirds of the members, stockholders, or delegates voting thereon at a meeting held after due written notice, setting forth the proposed action and the purpose of the meeting.</form.text></form.para>

Corp. Law &sect;16</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|25|32:25"><para.text>For an agricultural cooperative corporation, the bylaws may provide for their amendment by the board of directors, but any amendment adopted by the board that affects the preferential rights or obligations of the members or stockholders shall be reported to the next annual meeting of the corporation and, if not affirmatively approved thereat, shall cease to be in effect. Such bylaws reported to the annual meeting may be adopted, repealed, or amended on the affirmative vote of two-thirds of the members, stockholders, or delegates voting thereon at a meeting held after due written notice setting forth the proposed action and the purpose of the meeting. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="111">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;111</cite>.</para.text></para>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:26</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Waiver of requirements as to call, notice, and the like for board meetings</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia397cdf0181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><form.text>Directors may waive any and all provisions of law and/or of these bylaws in respect of call, notice, and place of meeting, or any of them, and may consent to the holding of any meeting without call and notice, or either of them, and without regard to the place where held. Any director may waive call, notice, and place of meeting, or any of them, in respect of himself or herself and may consent to the holding of any meeting without call and notice, or either of them, and without regard to the place where held.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><form.text>Any regular or special meeting of directors, held with unanimous consent or approval of all the shareholders of the board and attended by not less than a quorum, shall be valid without regard to call and notice, or either of them, and without regard to the place where held. The proceedings of any such meeting shall be valid and constitute the act or acts of the board of directors as fully and conclusively as though taken at a meeting duly called and noticed and held at the place duly appointed. Attendance at and participation in the proceedings of any meeting, attended and participated in by not less than a quorum, without objection to the regularity or sufficiency of, or lack of, call and notice, or either, or the place where held, shall constitute and be a waiver in respect of such matters and an irrevocable consent to the holding of such meeting on the part of and by the director so attending and participating without objection.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><form.text>The waiver and consent of any director who is not present at such meeting may be made or given either before, during, or after the meeting and may be made and evidenced:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><form.text>In writing, filed with the secretary, either before, during, or after the meeting;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><form.text>By subscribing at the foot of the minutes of the meeting an approval of such minutes; or</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(3)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><form.text>By approving, without objection, the minutes of the meeting at a subsequent meeting of the board, attended by the director who was absent from the first-mentioned meeting and whose waiver of consent is to be secured.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><para.text>One of the meetings of the corporation must be designated as the annual meeting. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-buscorp" secref="602" subref="(c)">BCL &sect;602(c)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|26|32:26"><para.text>Waiver of notice of director&apos;s meetings is authorized by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-buscorp" secref="711" subref="(c)">BCL &sect;711(c)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:27</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Voting rights, distributions, and disposition of membership</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia397f500181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|27|32:27"><form.text>Each member shall be entitled to one vote regardless of the number of shares owned. The cooperative&apos;s net income derived from business with or for the members shall be allocated and distributed as patronage dividends to them in proportion to the relative amount of business done with or for each member. Patronage dividends will be distributed either in cash or in the form of qualified checks, as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="1388" subref="(b)">Internal Revenue Code &sect;1388(b)</cite>, no later than the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of the <inline.instr>&lsqb;quarter/fiscal quarter/year&rsqb;</inline.instr> following the year in which earnings are derived. Dividends attributable to any nonpatronage income from business done with nonmembers, when distributed, will be distributed to the members in proportion to historical patronage.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|27|32:27"><form.text>Members shall not be permitted to sell their interest in the cooperative except to new members in connection with the admission of such new members or to the cooperative in connection with the withdrawal or expulsion of a member or for purposes of balancing ownership interests of the cooperative. If additional members are admitted to join the cooperative, pursuant to approval by a majority of existing members, the new member will be required to contribute cash as working capital to the cooperative in an amount determined by the members to be proportionate with the relative value of stock received and in relation to anticipated patronage by the new member.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|27|32:27"><para.text>For a discussion of considerations to be taken into account when drafting bylaws of a cooperative, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="32:11">&sect;32:11</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<form uuid="Ia3984320181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|29|32:29"><form.text>Directors shall receive no stated salary for their services as directors, but each director shall be paid for each regular or special meeting the sum of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of compensation&rsqb;</inline.instr> or such further sum as the members may fix from time to time at any meeting of the board. A director shall be allowed reasonable expenses while engaged in the business of the cooperative, to be audited, allowed, and paid as other claims against the cooperative. No director shall be appointed or employed by the cooperative for any position or in any capacity for which he or she shall be paid a salary or other remuneration for more than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days&apos; work in any one year, exclusive of the compensation and expenses to be paid for attendance at directors&apos; meetings.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|29|32:29"><para.text>A corporation may provide a fair remuneration for its officers and directors and for members of its executive committee. No officer or director or member of the executive committee may be a party to a contract for profit with the corporation that in any way differs from similar contracts with members or with others or that varies from terms generally current in the district. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="62">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;62</cite>.</para.text></para>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia3986a30181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|30|32:30"><form.text>Each person who hereafter applies for and is accepted to membership in this corporation, and each member of this corporation on the effective date of this article of the bylaws of the corporation who continues as a member after such date shall, by such act alone, consent that the amount of any distribution of patronage dividends <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="1388" subref="(a)">Section 1388(a) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite>&rsqb;</inline.instr> and the amount of any distribution of the kind referred to in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="1382" subref="(c)" pararef="(2)" spararef="(A)">Section 1382(c)(2)(A) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> occurring after <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of date&rsqb;</inline.instr>, which distributions are made in written notices of allocation as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="1388" subref="(b)">Section 1388(b) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> and which are received by such person from the corporation, will be taken into account by such person at their stated dollar amount in the manner provided in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="1385" subref="(a)">Section 1385(a) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> in the taxable year in which such written notices of allocation are received by such person.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|30|32:30"><para.text>This bylaw provision is included to qualify the written notices of allocation of the corporation and is substantially in the form found in the regulations. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.1388-1" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)" spararef="(ii)" clref="(b)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.1388-1(c)(3)(ii)(b)</cite>. For the bylaw to be effective, the patron must receive written notification and a copy of the bylaw provision.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|30|32:30"><para.text>For the bylaw to be effective, the patron must receive a written notification and copy of the bylaw. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1388" subref="(c)" pararef="(2)" spararef="(B)" clref="(ii)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;1388(c)(2)(B)(ii)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:31</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Election of directors by district</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia3989140181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Election Districts.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|32|32:31"><form.text>The territory in which the corporation has members shall be divided into districts. Unless and until changed as herein provided, there shall be <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of districts&rsqb;</inline.instr> districts, and the respective districts and their boundaries shall be those established by resolution of the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Change of Election Districts.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|32|32:31"><form.text>By resolution adopted by majority vote, the board of directors may, from time to time: (a) without affecting the number of districts, change the boundaries of one or more districts by adding to it territory not included up to that time within any district or by adding to one district territory theretofore embraced within another or by excluding from a district a part of its territories; or (b) change the number of districts by redistricting the entire territory, discontinuing a district, or merging a district with one or more districts or by any other means.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Election of Directors by District and At-Large.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|32|32:31"><form.text>There shall be as many directors as there are districts, one director to be elected by the members of each district, provided, however, that when the number of districts is an even number, there shall be one additional director to be known as a director-at-large and to be elected by all members of the corporation. Each director must be a member of the corporation and engaged in <inline.instr>&lsqb;description of activity&rsqb;</inline.instr> on a commercial scale or must be the authorized representative of a member so engaged if the latter is not a single natural person. A district director must be a resident of the district in which he or she is elected or for which he or she is appointed.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Effect on Tenure of Directors by Change in Districts.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|32|32:31"><form.text>Whenever a district is discontinued, the director representing that district shall cease to be a director and the office shall be discontinued. Whenever a new district is created, a director to represent it shall be selected in the manner herein provided in case of a vacancy. The same procedure is applicable when the creation of a new district necessitates the selection of a director-at-large. Notwithstanding the simultaneous discontinuance and creation of districts, if a director-at-large is still necessary as before such changes, the person then serving as such director shall continue to hold that office, subject to any other relevant provisions of the bylaws. Any question as to the effect of any changes made as herein provided in district boundaries or the number or identity of districts shall be conclusively determined by the board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Nomination of Directors.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|32|32:31"><form.text>Nominations for directors, either at-large or for a district, shall be made by petition addressed to the secretary of the corporation requesting that the secretary place upon the ballot the name of the person so nominated. Such a petition nominating a director-at-large shall be signed by not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;fraction of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members of the corporation. Such a petition nominating a district director shall be signed by not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;fraction of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> of members from that district.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|32|32:31"><para.text>Election of directors according to territorial districts is provided for in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="61">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;61</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>

<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="128">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;128</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="129">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;129</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="545">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;545</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:32</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Treatment of losses</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia398df60181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|33|32:32"><form.text>In the event of a substantial loss to the corporation from any cause whatsoever, the board of directors may, in its discretion, charge all or a part of such loss to current operating expenses. Any part of such loss not charged to current operating expenses (up to the whole amount of such loss) may, in the board&apos;s discretion, be: (1) charged ratably and proportionately against revolving fund credits for the year during which the loss occurred; or (2) charged ratably and proportionately against all revolving fund credits (for all years), in which event such loss may be apportioned between revolving funds.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|33|32:32"><form.text>In the event any loss is charged against revolving fund credits, such credit shall be reduced by its proportionate part of the loss and the records pertaining to the revolving fund changed accordingly. Notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained elsewhere in these bylaws, there shall be payable in respect to any credit against which a loss has been charged only the difference between the amount of the credit as originally entered and the portion of the loss charged to such credit.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|33|32:32"><form.text>The board of directors shall have power to determine when a substantial loss has occurred, and its determination shall be conclusive. In making such determination, the board may consider losses from bank suspension, uncollected accounts, fire, explosion, accident, or other calamity and losses arising from any other source or for any other reason.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|33|32:32"><para.text>A revolving fund operates to retain the capital of a cooperative; members of the cooperative are credited with their proportionate part of the fund. See <cite type="secondary" normalpub="aj2" topicname="Cooperative Associations" secref="22">Am. Jur. 2d, Cooperative Associations &sect;22</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Agriculture" numref="6">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Agriculture &key;6</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="128">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;128</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="129">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;129</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="alr3" titlename="Co-operative associations: rights in equity credits or patronage dividends" volref="50" pageref="435">Co-operative associations: rights in equity credits or patronage dividends, 50 A.L.R.3d 435</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="245">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;245</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>

Should the Cooperative not desire to repurchase such stock of a deceased member it may be sold or transferred to any other person eligible for membership in the Corporation as set forth in these bylaws.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|34|32:33"><form.text>The board of directors shall not buy the member&apos;s stock for more than par value.</form.text></form.para>

<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:35</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Expulsion and withdrawal</name></outline.name.block>

<form uuid="Ia3995490181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|36|32:35"><form.text>The board of directors may prefer charges against any member in accordance with the bylaws if the board determines that such member has ceased to be a bona fide producer of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of product&rsqb;</inline.instr>, has violated any of the provisions of the bylaws or of the contract with the corporation, or has been guilty of conduct detrimental to the corporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|36|32:35"><form.text>Any member may withdraw from the corporation by giving <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days&apos; notice in writing to the directors, but such withdrawal shall not affect any right or lien that the corporation has against the retiring member or the member&apos;s property until the indebtedness to the corporation is fully paid. If such notice is not given, it shall be assumed that each member desires to continue membership.</form.text></form.para>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:36</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Expulsion of member; Procedure</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia3997ba0181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|37|32:36"><form.text>Members may be expelled from membership for breach of contract or for acts injurious to the association.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|37|32:36"><form.text>Any member of this association may be expelled by a resolution passed and adopted at any meeting of the members called for the purpose or at any regular meeting, the reason for expulsion being stated in the resolution.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|37|32:36"><form.text>Three members of the board of directors or any officer shall notify the accused member, in writing, of the charge at least 15 days before the date of a proposed meeting when the charges shall be considered by the board of directors. Upon the affirmative vote of two-thirds of the directors and upon the recommendation of three executive officers, if any, of the member&apos;s respective district organization, which decision shall be final, the person so accused shall be denied further benefit of membership privileges except to conclude unfinished transactions.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|37|32:36"><form.text>The expelled member shall have his or her property interest in the association equitably and fairly appraised by the board of directors and the amount fixed in money within <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days after the close of the season in which expelled, and there shall be paid to the member the amount of the appraisal as and when the same would have been paid had the person remained a member of the association. Furthermore, the appraisal of the interest of the member as made by the board of directors shall be conclusive and binding.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|37|32:36"><para.text>In accordance with provisions in the bylaws, any person shall forfeit his or her membership upon proof that he or she has ceased to be engaged in the occupation or occupations for the servicing of which the corporation was formed or has ceased to have the qualifications requisite for membership and shall, upon such notice and terms as may be prescribed in the bylaws, surrender his or her membership certificate or his or her shares of stock upon payment of the par or otherwise designated value thereof and of any accrued dividends thereon, as may appear in the accounting at the end of the current fiscal year. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="42">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;42</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Agriculture" numref="6">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Agriculture &key;6</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>

</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:37</designator><name>Bylaw provision<sep/>Distribution on dissolution</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>REO</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia399a2b0181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|39|32:37"><form.text>On dissolution of this corporation, all debts and liabilities of the corporation shall be paid first according to their respective priorities. Any property remaining after discharge of the corporation&apos;s debts and liabilities shall be distributed to the shareholders and patrons. Holders of shares of preferred stock shall first be paid and shall be limited to the par value of their preferred shares, plus any dividends declared thereon and unpaid. Holders of shares of common stock shall next be paid and shall be limited to the par value of their common shares. Holders of credits in the revolving fund shall then be paid in the amount of their credit in the fund. The remainder of the property shall be distributed among the patrons who have patronized the corporation during the <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of fiscal years&rsqb;</inline.instr> fiscal years immediately preceding the dissolution, on the basis of their respective patronage as shown by the corporation&apos;s records.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|39|32:37"><para.text>A cooperative corporation may, at any meeting and upon due and express notice previously given, by vote of two-thirds of all of the members or stockholders voting thereon, discontinue its operations and settle its affairs. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="17">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;17</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>On convening, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of temporary chairperson&rsqb;</inline.instr> was elected temporary chairperson and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of temporary secretary&rsqb;</inline.instr> temporary secretary of the meeting, and each assumed <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her&rsqb;</inline.instr> office.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>The chair called for proof of notice of the meeting, whereupon <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of person presenting waiver of notice&rsqb;</inline.instr> presented a waiver of notice and consent to hold the meeting, signed by all the directors of the corporation, which waiver and consent was in the following form: <inline.instr>&lsqb;recitation of waiver of notice and consent to holding of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>On roll call of the directors of the corporation, the following answered present: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of all directors present&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>The chair ruled that proper and legal notice of the meeting had been given and that a quorum was present and announced that the meeting was opened for the transaction of business.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>The chair stated that the meeting was called for the purpose of electing corporate officers for the ensuing year and for the transaction of any other business that might properly come before the meeting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>On motion duly made and seconded, the following officers were unanimously elected to serve at the board&apos;s discretion until the time of the board&apos;s first regular meeting, to be held as soon as practicable following the first annual shareholder&apos;s meeting: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of officers elected&rsqb;</inline.instr> and <inline.instr>&lsqb;titles of officers elected&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>Following the election of officers, the president took the chair, and the secretary assumed <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her&rsqb;</inline.instr> duties as secretary on the meeting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>On motion duly made, seconded, and carried, the following resolution was adopted:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>Resolved, that <inline.instr>&lsqb;recitation of text resolution&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>

<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|43|32:41"><form.text>There being no further business to come before the meeting, on motion duly made, seconded, and unanimously adopted, the meeting was adjourned.</form.text></form.para>
