<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia39e5da0181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>Agreement made <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of agreement&rsqb;</inline.instr>, between <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of distributor&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a distributor of dairy products having <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her/its&rsqb;</inline.instr> principal office at <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of distributor&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, State of New York, referred to as &ldquo;Distributor,&rdquo; and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a cooperative corporation organized and existing under the laws of the State of New York, referred to as &ldquo;Corporation.&rdquo;</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>1</designator><name>PURCHASE OF DAIRY PRODUCTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>Distributor agrees to buy <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her/its&rsqb;</inline.instr> entire supply of <inline.instr>&lsqb;description of products&rsqb;</inline.instr>, excluding <inline.instr>&lsqb;list of exclusions&rsqb;</inline.instr>, from or through corporation, and corporation agrees to supply Distributor with all such products during the period and on the terms and conditions stated in this agreement.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>Distributor may select from among the members of corporation those members whose products <inline.instr>&lsqb;he/she&rsqb;</inline.instr> desires to buy under this contract. Subject to the prior consent and approval of the board of directors of corporation, the selected members may then deliver such products directly to Distributor.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>2</designator><name>PRICES</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>Distributor shall pay to corporation for all dairy products sold and delivered to <inline.instr>&lsqb;him/her&rsqb;</inline.instr> by or through corporation not less than the minimum class prices set forth in the marketing agreement and order for the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of marketing area&rsqb;</inline.instr> marketing area, State of New York, which <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: agreement was approved by &lsqb;name of approver&rsqb; and&rsqb;</inline.instr> became effective <inline.instr>&lsqb;effective date of agreement&rsqb;</inline.instr>, and all amendments thereto. A copy of that marketing agreement and order is attached and made a part of this contract. Any new marketing order or amendment to the present order that affects this contract will become effective as to this contract when such new agreement or amendment becomes effective. If the present marketing agreement and order is terminated and not immediately replaced by a new agreement and order, the price to be paid for dairy products sold and delivered under this contract will be mutually agreed on between the parties to this contract.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>3</designator><name>INABILITY TO PERFORM</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>In case of any cause beyond the control of either party that shall render it impossible for corporation to deliver or Distributor to handle or dispose of dairy products to be sold or received under this agreement, no liability for nonperformance of this agreement caused hereby will be incurred during the existence of that cause. In the case of a short supply of the dairy products covered by this agreement, corporation agrees to prorate its production on a percentage of sales basis with every buyer of dairy products. In the case of its inabilities to supply dairy products from locally purchased sources, corporation will attempt to purchase such products for Distributor&apos;s account from outside sources.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>4</designator><name>ACCOUNTS, RECORDS, AND INSPECTIONS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>Distributor agrees to keep complete and accurate records and accounts of all dairy products received by <inline.instr>&lsqb;him/her&rsqb;</inline.instr> or at <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her/its&rsqb;</inline.instr> plant during the term of this agreement, showing the source, quality, quantity, and disposition thereof, with dates, together with accurate summaries thereof, and to render such accounts and records to corporation at the time of or prior to the settlement of accounts between the parties. Corporation will have full opportunity to check the sufficiency and accuracy of such records, accounts, and summaries and shall be permitted to have one or more representatives on the premises of Distributor where such dairy products are received, handled, processed, and prepared for sale and delivery at all times, with authority to take inventories; to examine the salespersons&apos; daily load and return sheets and all other records and memoranda covering road sales; to check samples of cream; and to take samples of milk and cream from any cans or containers on the premises.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>5</designator><name>BUTTERFAT TESTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>The payment for all milk will be based on the average of not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of separate butterfat tests&rsqb;</inline.instr> separate butterfat tests of each producer&apos;s delivery during each month, conducted by an independent laboratory acceptable to Distributor and corporation. Corporation and Distributor will each pay one-half of the cost of such tests. Both Distributor and corporation agree to accept as final the average of the <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of samples&rsqb;</inline.instr> samples taken by the laboratory as a basis of settlement. Corporation may check weights and butterfat tests at Distributor&apos;s plant at all times.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>6</designator><name>ACCOUNTING AND PAYMENT</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>Distributor will render to corporation not later than the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of each month an accounting of all dairy products purchased during the preceding month. Payment for all such dairy products will be made directly to corporation daily on estimates furnished by corporation, subject to adjustment based on complete billing at the end of the month. Any underpayment or overpayment resulting from such daily payments as compared to the total billing for the month will be made good by the party liable therefor immediately on notice of such liability. Final adjustment as a result of ordered adjustment of receipts at sale shall be settled immediately on determination of the ordered adjustment.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>7</designator><name>EFFECTIVE DATE AND DURATION</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>This agreement will become effective on <inline.instr>&lsqb;effective date of agreement&rsqb;</inline.instr> and shall continue until terminated by either party on <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr>-days written notice of cancellation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><form.text>In witness, the parties have executed this agreement at <inline.instr>&lsqb;place of execution&rsqb;</inline.instr> the day and year first written above.</form.text></form.para>

<item.reference.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|55|32:53"><para.text>Under the New York Uniform Commercial Code, as under prior statutory and case law, the parties, if they so intend, can conclude a contract for sale even though the price is not settled. Where not settled by the agreement, the price to be paid is a reasonable price at the time for delivery if: (a) nothing is said as to price; (b) the price is left to be agreed by the parties and they fail to agree; or (c) the price is to be fixed in terms of some agreed market or other standard as set or recorded by a third person or agency and it is not so set or recorded. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-ucc" secref="2-305">NYUCC &sect;2-305</cite>.</para.text></para>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:54</designator><name>Terms concerning delivery of product</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>

<form uuid="Ia39eabc0181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|56|32:54"><form.text>All products will be delivered by producer at the earliest reasonable time when ready and, in any event, prior to the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> in each year, as and where directed by corporation. Where the packing plants of the corporation or its subsidiary are distant from the common delivery point, corporation may, in its discretion, assume the cost of transportation from the common shipping point to its packing plant. However, the delivery will not be deemed to have been made under this agreement except at the plant or grading points designated by corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|56|32:54"><form.text>Any deduction, charge, or loss that corporation may make or suffer because of inferior grade, quality, or condition of products will be charged against the producer individually.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|56|32:54"><form.text>Corporation will make rules and regulations regarding handling and delivering and will provide inspectors and graders to standardize, grade, and classify products; producer agrees to observe and to perform any such rules and regulations and to accept the grading and standards established by corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>d</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|56|32:54"><form.text>All products will be delivered in merchantable condition. The corporation&apos;s determination as to grade, standard, and classification and differentials in prices will be conclusive.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>e</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|56|32:54"><form.text>All products delivered under this agreement will be produced in compliance with the requirements of the Fair Labor Standards Act, as amended, and all regulations and orders of the U.S. Department of Labor issued thereunder, and with the requirements of any applicable New York authority or other applicable acts and all regulations and orders issued thereunder.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>f</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|56|32:54"><form.text>Producer guarantees all products, deliverable under this contract as of the date of shipment or delivery to be on such date, not adulterated or misbranded within the meaning of the Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act and not an article that may not, under the provisions of the Act (as the same now exists or may hereafter be amended), be introduced into interstate commerce.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>

<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|56|32:54"><para.text>If this provision is part of a contract of sale, the provisions of the New York UCC would apply concerning the place and time of delivery. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-ucc" secref="2-101 et seq." secrange="y">NYUCC &dblsect;2-101 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>

<form uuid="Ia39ef9e0181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|59|32:56"><form.text>Except as provided in subsection (b) of this section, corporation shall, by right of subrogation, have all rights, privileges, and benefits accruing to producer as a result of transactions between producer and any dealer to whom products covered by this agreement are sold. Any person, firm, or corporation receiving such products from producer, after notice, will make payment to corporation of all money due or to become due producer for any such products as may be demanded by corporation. Any person, firm, or corporation continuing to receive such products after notice of the execution of this agreement will be deemed to accept them subject to the terms and conditions of this agreement, and any such products sold or delivered by producer to any person, firm, or corporation, whether in violation of the terms and provisions of this agreement or not, will be sold subject to this agreement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|59|32:56"><form.text>If producer is offered a direct contract for such products, producer will immediately report such offer in writing to corporation. Corporation may permit members to contract for the sale of products for limited periods directly to dealers distributors or other purchasers designated by corporation, but only on such terms and conditions as are authorized by corporation in writing and provided that corporation is guaranteed full and prompt payment of all deductions authorized by this agreement or by the bylaws and rules of corporation with respect to such direct sales.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|59|32:56"><form.text>In the event of the failure of any dealer or other purchaser mentioned in subsection (a) or (b) of this section to deliver the products or the proceeds from their sale, as set forth above, producer will be obligated to corporation for liquidated damages herein provided on the basis of the amount of products covered directly or indirectly by such transfer, in addition to the other remedies granted in this agreement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:58</designator><name>Liquidated damages for nondelivery or wrongful delivery; percentage of market value</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia39f4800181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|61|32:58"><form.text>Producer agrees to pay to corporation as liquidated damages for all products sold, delivered, or withheld by or for the producer, other than in accordance with the terms of this agreement, <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of liquidated damages&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the total market value of such products. Market value is to be determined as of the time that demand for shipment of the products is made by corporation. If the products have been sold by producer, then the price for which the products have been sold will be their market value.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|61|32:58"><para.text>The marketing agreement may fix specific sums as liquidated damages, which sums will not be regarded as penalties, payable for breach by a member or shareholder or contracting nonmember of the marketing obligation. A provision of this type may also be placed in the certificate of incorporation or bylaws. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-coopcorp" secref="70" subref="(2)">Coop. Corp. Law &sect;70(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:59</designator><name>Payment and deductions from sale of pooled products; advances</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia39f9620181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|62|32:59"><form.text>Corporation agrees to resell such products of producer as may be pooled, together with products of like quality, grade, and classification delivered by other growers under substantially similar contracts, at the best prices obtainable under market conditions and to pay over the net amount received therefrom as payment in full to producer and producers named in contracts substantially similar to this agreement, according to the value of the products delivered by each producer after deducting therefrom the cost of receiving, handling, packing, manufacturing, storing, depreciation, advertising, and marketing and an investment charge not to exceed <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of gross resale proceeds&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the gross resale proceeds. From this charge, a commercial reserve may be created and deductions made for the creation of the capital funds of corporation, provided for by the bylaws thereof. The annual surplus from any deductions made by corporation and not prorated to any specific fund must be prorated among the producers delivering products in that year on the basis of their respective deliveries.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|62|32:59"><form.text>Corporation agrees to pay an advance payment on the products as substantial as the market and financial conditions will permit, as determined by the board of directors in each season. Such payment will be made as soon as practicable after delivery of the products to corporation. Such advance payment may be proportionately higher for products classified in the more desirable grades or sizes from a commercial standpoint.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|62|32:59"><form.text>Payment on each pool will be made from time to time, as rapidly as possible, in due proportion, until the accounts of each pool of the season are completely settled.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|62|32:59"><para.text>If a buyer&ndash;-seller relationship exists between the cooperative and the patron, advance payments will have to be taken into income when received. If the relationship is that of principal and agent, however, the advances may be considered as loans and not taxed until the cooperative, as agent, realizes income for the patron, as principal. The appropriate status cannot be determined from the provisions of the above form; the other terms of the agreement would be needed to make that determination.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Agriculture" numref="6">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Agriculture &key;6</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="128">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;128</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="129">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;129</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>32:60</designator><name>Reference to bylaw respecting tax treatment of patronage dividend allocation</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ia39fbd30181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|63|32:60"><form.text>Producer acknowledges that, prior to the execution of this agreement, producer was advised and understands that the corporation has adopted a bylaw reading as follows: <inline.instr>&lsqb;text of bylaw provision concerning tax treatment of patronage dividend to allocations&rsqb;</inline.instr> <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: and that &lsqb;name of regional exchange&rsqb; has adopted a similar bylaw&rsqb;</inline.instr>. Producer also acknowledges that, prior to the execution of this agreement, producer received and has read a letter notifying producer that the bylaw above referred to has been adopted by corporation <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: and by &lsqb;name of regional exchange&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr> and of its significance, as required by the Internal Revenue Code and the regulations issued thereunder by the Internal Revenue Service, Department of the Treasury.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|63|32:60"><para.text>Among the many requirements imposed on cooperatives is that of giving notification regarding distributions to the patrons. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="1388" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;1388(a)(2)</cite>. The usual manner of handling this is to incorporate a provision into the bylaws similar to the above and then giving patrons a copy of the bylaw along with the letter of notification described. This must be done before a contract is entered into because, under the Code, the obligation to pay patronage dividends must have existed before the organization received the amount so paid, meaning before the transaction is entered into with the patron.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|63|32:60"><para.text>The need for the bylaw to which reference is made in this provision arises with respect to qualified written notices of allocation. See <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="32:6">&sect;32:6</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Agriculture" numref="6">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Agriculture &key;6</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="128">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;128</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Associations" numref="129">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Associations &key;129</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Qualified written notice of allocation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="E-1121">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d &para;E-1121</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Noncash patronage dividends, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="5:18">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;5:18</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<form uuid="Ia3a00b50181a11e68738d3db3a7c8dd3">
<form.para ct.id="6d0bf250b92611ef8747b569df12a67d|64|32:61"><form.text>Corporation agrees to buy and producer agrees to sell and deliver to corporation all of the products produced or acquired by or for producer in New York during the years <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of year 1&rsqb;</inline.instr> to <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of year 2&rsqb;</inline.instr> inclusive. This agreement may be terminated at any time during any year after <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of year&rsqb;</inline.instr> by corporation or by producer by a notice mailed to producer or corporation by registered mail between the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> and the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> days of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> of that year. Such termination will take effect on the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> of the year in which such notice is delivered, provided, however, that this agreement will remain in full force and effect as to all products delivered to corporation prior to such termination and until the sale of such products and payment of the proceeds thereof to producer. Notice must be mailed within the period named in this agreement to be effective and will be mailed to corporation at its personal place of business and to producer at producer&apos;s last-known address.</form.text></form.para>

Producer acknowledges that corporation has or will become a member of such central sales agency and has or will contract with the central sales agency to deliver all of the products handled by it to the central sales agency for packing and marketing. Producer agrees that corporation may contract with the central sales agency for these purposes and may agree to pool the products delivered under this agreement with products of a similar grade and quality delivered by similar corporations under marketing agreements substantially similar to this; the proceeds of this agreement will be divided ratably according to deliveries from such corporations and will be distributed to the grower members as above provided.</form.text></form.para>
